810:              const parseVerbDbPayload = (raw) => {
811:                  const txt = String(raw || '').trim();
812:                  if (!txt) return null;
813:                  const tryParse = (s) => { try { return JSON.parse(s); } catch (e) { return null; } };
814:                  let data = tryParse(txt);
815:                  if (!data && txt.startsWith('{') && txt.endsWith(']')) data = tryParse(txt + '\n}');
816:                  if (!data && txt.startsWith('"id"')) data = tryParse('[{' + txt + '}]');
817:                  if (!data) return null;
818:                  const verbs = Array.isArray(data) ? data : (Array.isArray(data.verbs) ? data.verbs : []);
819:                  if (!verbs.length) return null;
820:                  return { meta: data.meta || null, verbs };
821:              };
822:              const loadVerbDb = async () => {
823:                  const urls = [
824:                      `${GIST_VERB_DB}?nocache=${Date.now()}`,
825:                      './verbos-db.json'
826:                  ];
827:                  for (const u of urls) {
828:                      try {
829:                          const r = await fetch(u, { cache: 'no-cache' });
830:                          if (!r.ok) continue;
831:                          const raw = await r.text();
832:                          const parsed = parseVerbDbPayload(raw);
833:                          if (!parsed || !parsed.verbs.length) continue;
834:                          if (cancelled) return;
835:                          setRutaVerbDb(parsed);
836:                          return;
837:                      } catch (e) {}
838:                  }
839:              };
840:              loadVerbDb();
841:              return () => { cancelled = true; };
842:          }, []);

1937:const startPlacementTest = () => {
1938:  const initialQuestions = selectQuestionsForLevel('A2', 5);
1939:  setPlacementQuestions(initialQuestions);
1940:  setPlacementAnswers(new Array(initialQuestions.length).fill(null));

1946:
1947:const selectQuestionsForLevel = (level, count) => {
1948:  const allQuestions = window.MULLER_PLACEMENT_QUESTIONS || [];
1949:  const levelQuestions = allQuestions.filter(q => q.level === level);
1950:  const shuffled = [...levelQuestions].sort(() => Math.random() - 0.5);
1951:  return shuffled.slice(0, Math.min(count, levelQuestions.length));
1952:};
1953:
1954:const handlePlacementAnswer = (selectedOpt) => {
1955:  const currentQ = placementQuestions[placementIndex];
1956:  if (!currentQ) return;
1957:  
1958:  const isCorrect = (selectedOpt === currentQ.ok);
1959:  
1960:  // Actualizar respuestas
1961:  const newAnswers = [...placementAnswers];
1962:  newAnswers[placementIndex] = selectedOpt;
1963:  setPlacementAnswers(newAnswers);
1964:  
1965:  // Actualizar puntuación del nivel actual
1966:  const newScore = {
1967:    correct: placementScore.correct + (isCorrect ? 1 : 0),
1968:    total: placementScore.total + 1
1969:  };
1970:  setPlacementScore(newScore);
1971:  
1972:  // Reproducir sonido de acierto/fallo
1973:  if (window.__mullerNotifyExerciseOutcome) {
1974:    window.__mullerNotifyExerciseOutcome(isCorrect);
1975:  }
1976:  
1977:  // Lógica adaptativa
1978:  const performanceRatio = newScore.correct / newScore.total;
1979:  let nextLevel = placementLevel;
1980:  let shouldFinish = false;
1981:  
1982:  if (newScore.total >= 5) {
1983:    if (performanceRatio >= 0.7) {
1984:      // Buen rendimiento: subir de nivel
1985:      if (placementLevel === 'A1') nextLevel = 'A2';
1986:      else if (placementLevel === 'A2') nextLevel = 'B1';
1987:      else if (placementLevel === 'B1') nextLevel = 'B2';
1988:      else if (placementLevel === 'B2') shouldFinish = true;
1989:    } else if (performanceRatio <= 0.3) {
1990:      // Mal rendimiento: bajar de nivel
1991:      if (placementLevel === 'B2') nextLevel = 'B1';
1992:      else if (placementLevel === 'B1') nextLevel = 'A2';
1993:      else if (placementLevel === 'A2') nextLevel = 'A1';
1994:      else if (placementLevel === 'A1') shouldFinish = true;
1995:    } else {
1996:      // Rendimiento intermedio: continuar mismo nivel
1997:      if (newScore.total >= 8) shouldFinish = true;
1998:    }
1999:  }
2000:  
2001:  // Si no hay más preguntas del nivel, finalizar
2002:  if (placementIndex >= placementQuestions.length - 1) {
2003:    shouldFinish = true;
2004:  }
2005:  
2006:  if (shouldFinish) {
2007:    const recommendedLevel = calculateRecommendedLevel();
2008:    finishPlacementWithLevel(recommendedLevel);
2009:    return;
2010:  }
2011:  
2012:  if (nextLevel !== placementLevel) {
2013:    // Cambiar de nivel
2014:    const newQuestions = selectQuestionsForLevel(nextLevel, 5);
2015:    setPlacementQuestions(newQuestions);
2016:    setPlacementAnswers(new Array(newQuestions.length).fill(null));
2017:    setPlacementIndex(0);
2018:    setPlacementLevel(nextLevel);
2019:    setPlacementScore({ correct: 0, total: 0 });
2020:  } else {
2021:    // Siguiente pregunta mismo nivel
2022:    setPlacementIndex(placementIndex + 1);
2023:  }
2024:};
2025:
2026:const calculateRecommendedLevel = () => {
2027:  const ratio = placementScore.total > 0 ? placementScore.correct / placementScore.total : 0;
2028:  if (placementLevel === 'A1' && ratio >= 0.6) return 'A2';
2029:  if (placementLevel === 'A2' && ratio >= 0.6) return 'B1';
2030:  if (placementLevel === 'B1' && ratio >= 0.6) return 'B2';
2031:  return placementLevel;
2032:};
2033:
2034:const finishPlacementWithLevel = (finalLevel) => {
2035:  const levelIndexMap = { 'A1': 0, 'A2': 1, 'B1': 2, 'B2': 3 };
2036:  const suggestedIdx = levelIndexMap[finalLevel] || 0;
2037:  
2038:  const next = { ...rutaProgress, placementDone: true, suggestedLevelIdx: suggestedIdx };
2039:  if (typeof window.mullerRutaSave === 'function') window.mullerRutaSave(next);
2040:  setRutaProgress(next);
2041:  setRutaSubTab('camino');
2042:  
2043:  if (window.__mullerPlaySfx) window.__mullerPlaySfx('levelup');
2044:  
2045:  setCelebrationModal({
2046:    title: 'Test de nivel completado',
2047:    subtitle: `Nivel recomendado: ${finalLevel}`,
2048:    xp: 0,
2049:    coins: 20,
2050:    milestone: false,
2051:    placement: true
2052:  });
2053:  
2054:  saveProgress({
2055:    coins: userStats.coins + 20,
2056:    activityByDay: mergeActivityPoints(25)
2057:  });
2058:  
2059:  // Resetear test
2060:  setPlacementQuestions([]);
2061:  setPlacementAnswers([]);
2062:  setPlacementIndex(0);
2063:  setPlacementFinished(false);

2083:              const tol = Math.max(2, Math.floor(b.length / 5));
2084:              if (a === b || dist <= tol) { window.__mullerNotifyExerciseOutcome && window.__mullerNotifyExerciseOutcome(true); setRutaSpeakErr(''); return true; }
2085:              window.__mullerNotifyExerciseOutcome && window.__mullerNotifyExerciseOutcome(false);

2225:                  const pages = [];

2233:                          text = mullerPdfCleanText(raw);
2234:                      } catch (err) {}
2235:                      const firstSlice = text.slice(0, 400);
2236:                      const meta = mullerPdfGuessUnitLesson(firstSlice);
2237:                      pages.push({
2238:                          page: pageNum,
2239:                          unit: meta.unit,
2240:                          lesson: meta.lesson,
2241:                          text: text.slice(0, MULLER_PDF_STORED_TEXT_MAX),
2242:                          ocrPending: !text
2243:                      });
2244:                      if ((pageNum % MULLER_PDF_EXTRACT_YIELD_EVERY) === 0) {
2245:                          await new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, 0));
2246:                      }
2247:                  }
2248:                  const compactPages = pages.slice(0, MULLER_PDF_STORED_PAGES_MAX);
2249:                  const payload = {
2250:                      id: `pdf-${Date.now()}`,
2251:                      name: file.name || 'Libro PDF',
2252:                      size: file.size || 0,
2253:                      totalPages,
2254:                      pages: compactPages,
2255:                      importedAt: new Date().toISOString()
2256:                  };
2257:                  setPdfStudyDoc(payload);
2258:                  setPdfStudyPageIdx(0);
2259:                  try { localStorage.setItem(MULLER_PDF_STUDY_STORAGE_KEY, JSON.stringify(payload)); } catch (e) {}
2260:                  const extractedCount = compactPages.filter((p) => p.text).length;
2261:                  setPdfStudyBusyMsg(`PDF listo: ${extractedCount}/${compactPages.length} páginas con texto.`);
2262:              } catch (err) {
2263:                  setPdfStudyErr(err && err.message ? err.message : 'No se pudo leer el PDF.');
2264:              } finally {
2265:                  setPdfStudyExtracting(false);
2266:              }
2267:          }, []);
2268:
2269:          const runPdfPageOcr = useCallback(async (pageNumber) => {
2270:              if (!pdfStudyDoc) return;
2271:              const idx = Math.max(0, (Number(pageNumber) || 1) - 1);
2272:              const pages = Array.isArray(pdfStudyDoc.pages) ? pdfStudyDoc.pages : [];
2273:              const page = pages[idx];
2274:              if (!page) return;
2275:              if (page.text && page.text.length >= 40) {
2276:                  setPdfStudyBusyMsg('Esta página ya tiene texto; OCR no es necesario.');
2277:                  return;
2278:              }
2279:              const ocrReady = await mullerEnsureTesseractLoaded().catch(() => false);
2280:              if (!ocrReady || typeof Tesseract === 'undefined') {
2281:                  setPdfStudyErr('No se pudo cargar OCR (Tesseract).');
2282:                  return;
2283:              }
2284:              const pdfReady = await mullerEnsurePdfJsLoaded().catch(() => false);
2285:              if (!pdfReady || !window.pdfjsLib || typeof window.pdfjsLib.getDocument !== 'function') {
2286:                  setPdfStudyErr('OCR PDF no disponible en este navegador.');
2287:                  return;
2288:              }
2289:              if (!pdfStudyBufferRef.current && !pdfStudyDocHandleRef.current) {
2290:                  setPdfStudyErr('Para OCR real de página, vuelve a subir el PDF en esta sesión.');
2291:                  setPdfStudyBusyMsg('OCR no disponible: falta el PDF en memoria.');
2292:                  return;
2293:              }
2294:              setPdfStudyOcrBusy(true);
2295:              let worker = null;
2296:              let attemptNo = 0;
2297:              const attemptCap = 1 + Math.max(0, Number(MULLER_PDF_OCR_RETRY_MAX) || 0);
2298:              try {
2299:                  setPdfStudyErr('');
2300:                  const safePage = Math.max(1, Number(page.page || pageNumber) || 1);
2301:                  while (attemptNo < attemptCap) {
2302:                      try {
2303:                          setPdfStudyBusyMsg(`Preparando OCR página ${safePage}${attemptNo > 0 ? ` (reintento ${attemptNo}/${attemptCap - 1})` : ''}…`);
2304:                          window.pdfjsLib.GlobalWorkerOptions.workerSrc = MULLER_PDFJS_WORKER_URL;
2305:                          let pdf = pdfStudyDocHandleRef.current;
2306:                          if (!pdf) {
2307:                              pdf = await window.pdfjsLib.getDocument({ data: pdfStudyBufferRef.current }).promise;
2308:                              pdfStudyDocHandleRef.current = pdf;
2309:                          }
2310:                          const pg = await pdf.getPage(safePage);
2311:                          let ocrText = '';
2312:                          const scales = [1.6, 2.1];
2313:                          for (let attempt = 0; attempt < scales.length; attempt++) {
2314:                              const scale = scales[attempt];
2315:                              const viewport = pg.getViewport({ scale });
2316:                              const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
2317:                              canvas.width = Math.max(1, Math.floor(viewport.width));
2318:                              canvas.height = Math.max(1, Math.floor(viewport.height));
2319:                              const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
2320:                              if (!ctx) throw new Error('No se pudo crear el contexto de imagen para OCR.');
2321:                              await pg.render({ canvasContext: ctx, viewport }).promise;
2322:                              setPdfStudyBusyMsg(`OCR página ${safePage}: intento ${attempt + 1}/${scales.length}${attemptNo > 0 ? ` · retry ${attemptNo}` : ''}…`);
2323:                              worker = await Tesseract.createWorker('deu', 1, {
2324:                                  logger: (m) => {
2325:                                      if (m && m.status === 'recognizing text' && typeof m.progress === 'number') {
2326:                                          setPdfStudyBusyMsg(`OCR página ${safePage}: ${Math.round(100 * m.progress)}%`);
2327:                                      }
2328:                                  }
2329:                              });
2330:                              const result = await worker.recognize(canvas);
2331:                              await worker.terminate();
2332:                              worker = null;
2333:                              const raw = result && result.data ? result.data.text : '';
2334:                              ocrText = mullerPdfCleanText(raw);
2335:                              if (ocrText.length >= 24 || attempt === scales.length - 1) break;
2336:                          }
2337:                          if (!ocrText) {
2338:                              setPdfStudyErr('OCR sin texto. Prueba una página más nítida o con más contraste.');
2339:                              setPdfStudyBusyMsg(`OCR página ${safePage}: sin texto detectado.`);
2340:                              return;
2341:                          }
2342:                          const meta = mullerPdfGuessUnitLesson(ocrText.slice(0, 400));
2343:                          const nextPages = pages.map((p, pIdx) => {
2344:                              if (pIdx !== idx) return p;
2345:                              return {
2346:                                  ...p,
2347:                                  unit: p.unit || meta.unit,
2348:                                  lesson: p.lesson || meta.lesson,
2349:                                  text: ocrText.slice(0, MULLER_PDF_STORED_TEXT_MAX),
2350:                                  ocrPending: false,
2351:                                  ocrUpdatedAt: new Date().toISOString()
2352:                              };
2353:                          });
2354:                          const nextDoc = { ...pdfStudyDoc, pages: nextPages, updatedAt: new Date().toISOString() };
2355:                          setPdfStudyDoc(nextDoc);
2356:                          try { localStorage.setItem(MULLER_PDF_STUDY_STORAGE_KEY, JSON.stringify(nextDoc)); } catch (e) {}
2357:                          setPdfStudyBusyMsg(`OCR completado en página ${safePage}.`);
2358:                          return;
2359:                      } catch (attemptErr) {
2360:                          if (worker) {
2361:                              try { await worker.terminate(); } catch (e) {}
2362:                              worker = null;
2363:                          }
2364:                          attemptNo += 1;
2365:                          if (attemptNo >= attemptCap) throw attemptErr;
2366:                          setPdfStudyBusyMsg(`OCR página ${safePage}: error temporal, reintentando…`);
2367:                          await new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, 220));
2368:                      }
2369:                  }
2370:              } catch (err) {
2371:                  setPdfStudyErr(err && err.message ? err.message : 'Error al ejecutar OCR de página.');
2372:              } finally {
2373:                  if (worker) {
2374:                      try { await worker.terminate(); } catch (e) {}
2375:                  }
2376:                  setPdfStudyOcrBusy(false);
2377:              }
2378:          }, [pdfStudyDoc]);
2379:

2425:          const runPdfDidacticAnalysis = useCallback((pageNumber) => {
2426:              if (!pdfStudyDoc) return;
2427:              const idx = Math.max(0, (Number(pageNumber) || 1) - 1);
2428:              const page = pdfStudyDoc.pages && pdfStudyDoc.pages[idx];
2429:              const txt = page && page.text ? String(page.text).trim() : '';
2430:              if (!txt || txt.length < 40) {
2431:                  setPdfStudyBusyMsg('No hay texto suficiente en esta página. Ejecuta OCR o elige otra.');
2432:                  return;
2433:              }
2434:              const normalized = txt.replace(/\s+/g, ' ').trim();
2435:              const sentenceCandidates = normalized
2436:                  .split(/(?<=[.!?])\s+/)
2437:                  .map((s) => s.trim())
2438:                  .filter((s) => s.length >= 28 && s.length <= 180);
2439:              const phrases = Array.from(new Set(sentenceCandidates)).slice(0, 8);
2440:              const words = (normalized.toLowerCase().match(/[a-zäöüß]{4,}/g) || [])
2441:                  .filter((w) => !MULLER_PDF_DIDACTIC_STOPWORDS.has(w));
2442:              const freq = {};
2443:              words.forEach((w) => { freq[w] = (freq[w] || 0) + 1; });
2444:              const keywords = Object.entries(freq)
2445:                  .sort((a, b) => b[1] - a[1])
2446:                  .slice(0, 16)
2447:                  .map(([de, count]) => ({ de, es: '', count }));
2448:              const gaps = phrases.slice(0, 6).map((p, i) => {
2449:                  const tokens = p.match(/[A-Za-zÄÖÜäöüß]{4,}/g) || [];
2450:                  let answer = '';
2451:                  for (let t = tokens.length - 1; t >= 0; t--) {
2452:                      const candidate = String(tokens[t] || '').toLowerCase();
2453:                      if (candidate && !MULLER_PDF_DIDACTIC_STOPWORDS.has(candidate)) { answer = candidate; break; }
2454:                  }
2455:                  if (!answer && tokens[0]) answer = String(tokens[0]).toLowerCase();
2456:                  const prompt = answer ? p.replace(new RegExp(`\\b${answer}\\b`, 'i'), '_____') : p;
2457:                  return { id: `gap-${i + 1}`, prompt, answer };
2458:              });
2459:              const compQuestions = phrases.slice(0, 4).map((p, i) => ({
2460:                  id: `comp-${i + 1}`,
2461:                  q: `¿Qué idea principal expresa esta frase ${i + 1}?`,
2462:                  context: p
2463:              }));
2464:              const pack = {
2465:                  id: `pdf-did-${Date.now()}`,
2466:                  sourceDocId: pdfStudyDoc.id || '',
2467:                  sourceDocName: pdfStudyDoc.name || 'Libro PDF',
2468:                  page: page.page || (idx + 1),
2469:                  unit: page.unit || '',
2470:                  lesson: page.lesson || '',
2471:                  createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
2472:                  keywords,
2473:                  phrases,
2474:                  exercises: {
2475:                      gaps,
2476:                      dictation: phrases.slice(0, 5),
2477:                      comprehension: compQuestions,
2478:                      miniTelc: phrases.slice(0, 3)
2479:                  }
2480:              };
2481:              setPdfDidacticPack(pack);
2482:              setPdfStudyBusyMsg(`Análisis didáctico listo (página ${pack.page}): ${pack.keywords.length} palabras clave y ${pack.phrases.length} frases.`);
2483:          }, [pdfStudyDoc]);

2654:          const checkRutaPdfGap = useCallback(() => {

2659:              const exp = String(current.answer || '').trim().toLowerCase();

2661:                  setRutaPdfFeedback('Respuesta abierta: compara con la frase original.');
2662:                  return;
2663:              }
2664:              if (got === exp) {
2665:                  setRutaPdfFeedback('Correcto.');
2666:                  window.__mullerNotifyExerciseOutcome && window.__mullerNotifyExerciseOutcome(true);
2667:              } else {
2668:                  setRutaPdfFeedback(`No exacto. Esperado: ${exp}`);
2669:                  window.__mullerNotifyExerciseOutcome && window.__mullerNotifyExerciseOutcome(false);
2670:              }
2671:              const packId = String(rutaPdfPack.id || '');
2672:              if (!packId) return;
2673:              setRutaPdfCoachStats((prev) => {
2674:                  const base = prev && typeof prev === 'object' ? prev : {};
2675:                  const currentStats = base[packId] && typeof base[packId] === 'object' ? base[packId] : { attempts: 0, correct: 0, errorWords: {}, srs: [] };
2676:                  const nextErrorWords = { ...(currentStats.errorWords || {}) };
2677:                  if (got !== exp && exp) nextErrorWords[exp] = (nextErrorWords[exp] || 0) + 1;
2678:                  const nextSrs = Array.isArray(currentStats.srs) ? currentStats.srs.map((card) => {
2679:                      if (!card || String(card.de || '').toLowerCase() !== exp) return card;
2680:                      const isOk = got === exp;
2681:                      const nextBox = isOk ? Math.min(5, (Number(card.box) || 1) + 1) : 1;
2682:                      const nextDue = Date.now() + (isOk ? (nextBox * nextBox * 3600000) : 1800000);
2683:                      return { ...card, box: nextBox, dueAt: nextDue };
2684:                  }) : [];
2685:                  const next = {
2686:                      ...base,
2687:                      [packId]: {
2688:                          ...currentStats,
2689:                          attempts: (Number(currentStats.attempts) || 0) + 1,
2690:                          correct: (Number(currentStats.correct) || 0) + (got === exp ? 1 : 0),
2691:                          errorWords: nextErrorWords,
2692:                          srs: nextSrs,
2693:                          updatedAt: new Date().toISOString()
2694:                      }
2695:                  };
2696:                  try { localStorage.setItem(MULLER_PDF_COACH_STATS_KEY, JSON.stringify(next)); } catch (e) {}
2697:                  return next;
2698:              });
2699:          }, [rutaPdfPack, rutaPdfGapIdx, rutaPdfGapInput]);

2998:          const renderPdfOverlayPageAsync = useCallback(async (pageNum, tw, th) => {
2999:              if (tw < 16 || th < 16) return '';
3000:              const pdfReady = await mullerEnsurePdfJsLoaded().catch(() => false);
3001:              if (!pdfReady || !window.pdfjsLib) return '';

3003:                  window.pdfjsLib.GlobalWorkerOptions.workerSrc = MULLER_PDFJS_WORKER_URL;
3004:                  let pdf = pdfStudyDocHandleRef.current;

3006:                      pdf = await window.pdfjsLib.getDocument({ data: pdfStudyBufferRef.current }).promise;
3007:                      pdfStudyDocHandleRef.current = pdf;

3010:                  const page = await pdf.getPage(Math.max(1, Number(pageNum) || 1));
3011:                  const v0 = page.getViewport({ scale: 1 });
3012:                  const scale = Math.min(tw / v0.width, th / v0.height) * 0.994;
3013:                  const viewport = page.getViewport({ scale });
3014:                  const rc = document.createElement('canvas');
3015:                  rc.width = Math.max(1, Math.floor(viewport.width));

3017:                  const rctx = rc.getContext('2d', { alpha: false });
3018:                  if (!rctx) return '';
3019:                  rctx.fillStyle = '#f8fafc';
3020:                  rctx.fillRect(0, 0, rc.width, rc.height);
3021:                  const rt = page.render({ canvasContext: rctx, viewport });
3022:                  await (rt && rt.promise ? rt.promise : rt);
3023:                  const out = document.createElement('canvas');
3024:                  out.width = Math.floor(tw);
3025:                  out.height = Math.floor(th);
3026:                  const octx = out.getContext('2d', { alpha: false });
3027:                  if (!octx) return '';
3028:                  octx.fillStyle = '#f1f5f9';
3029:                  octx.fillRect(0, 0, out.width, out.height);
3030:                  const s = Math.min(tw / rc.width, th / rc.height);
3031:                  const dw = rc.width * s;
3032:                  const dh = rc.height * s;
3033:                  const ox = (tw - dw) / 2;
3034:                  const oy = (th - dh) / 2;
3035:                  octx.drawImage(rc, 0, 0, rc.width, rc.height, ox, oy, dw, dh);
3036:                  return out.toDataURL('image/png');
3037:              } catch (e) {
3038:                  return '';
3039:              }
3040:          }, []);

3632:                  const base = clean.slice(0, -2);
3633:                  return { touched: clean, infinitive: clean, forms: `Prät: ${base}te | Perf: hat ${clean} (regular estimado)` };

3858:  const handleSaveScript = () => {

3888:                        const cleanDe = parts[0].trim().replace(/[🔴🔵🟢•]/g, '');
3889:                        vocab.push({ de: cleanDe, es: parts[1].trim(), diff: 1 });
3890:                    }
3891:                });

3893:            }

3898:            if (transMatch) {
3899:                translation = transMatch[1].trim();
3900:                content = content.replace(transMatch[0], '').trim();
3901:            }

3905:

3921:                    new Request(new URL('./.muller-offline-meta.json', window.location.href).toString()),
3922:                    new Response(JSON.stringify(meta), { headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' } })

3930:    } catch (e) {

4530:              const pickAlt = (res) => {
4531:                  let alt = res[0];
4532:                  for (let j = 1; j < res.length; j++) {
4533:                      const cj = res[j].confidence;
4534:                      const cb = alt.confidence;
4535:                      if (typeof cj === 'number' && (typeof cb !== 'number' || cj >= cb)) alt = res[j];
4536:                  }
4537:                  return alt;
4538:              };
4539:              recognition.onstart = () => {

4547:              };
4548:              recognition.onresult = (event) => {
4549:                  const finals = [];
4550:                  let interim = "";
4551:                  for (let i = event.resultIndex; i < event.results.length; i++) {
4552:                      const res = event.results[i];
4553:                      const alt = pickAlt(res);
4554:                      const raw = (alt.transcript || "").trim();
4555:                      if (!raw) continue;
4556:                      if (res.isFinal) finals.push(raw);
4557:                      else interim = raw;
4558:                  }
4559:                  if (finals.length) {
4560:                      if (mobileStt) {
4561:                          if (finals.length === 1) {
4562:                              const f = finals[0];
4563:                              const cur = speechFinalRef.current || "";
4564:                              if (!cur) speechFinalRef.current = f;
4565:                              else if (f.startsWith(cur.trim())) speechFinalRef.current = f;
4566:                              else if (cur.startsWith(f) && f.length < cur.length) { /* mantener frase más larga */ }
4567:                              else if (f.length >= cur.length && (f.indexOf(cur) >= 0 || cur.indexOf(f) >= 0)) speechFinalRef.current = f.length >= cur.length ? f : cur;
4568:                              else speechFinalRef.current = mergeSpeechFinalChunk(cur, f);
4569:                          } else {
4570:                              const chunk = finals.join(" ").trim();
4571:                              speechFinalRef.current = mergeSpeechFinalChunk(speechFinalRef.current, chunk);
4572:                          }
4573:                      } else {
4574:                          for (const f of finals) {
4575:                              speechFinalRef.current = mergeSpeechFinalChunk(speechFinalRef.current, f);
4576:                          }
4577:                      }
4578:                  }

7600:                          </div>

7749:        // ========== COMPONENTES FLOTANTES (Sincronización y Permiso Micrófono) ==========
7750:        function FloatingButtons() {
7751:            const [lastBackupIso, setLastBackupIso] = React.useState(() => localStorage.getItem('muller_last_backup_iso'));
7752:
7753:            const requestMicPermission = async () => {
7754:                try {
7755:                    const ok = await window.mullerRequestMicPermission && window.mullerRequestMicPermission({ autoPrompt: true, showToast: true });
7756:                    if (!ok) return;
7757:                    window.__mullerToast && window.__mullerToast('Micrófono concedido. Ya puedes usar reconocimiento de voz.', 'success');
7758:                } catch (err) {
7759:                    window.__mullerToast && window.__mullerToast('No se pudo obtener permiso del micrófono.', 'error');
7760:                }
7761:            };
7762:
7763:            const exportData = React.useCallback(() => {
7764:                const allLocalData = {};
7765:                for (let i = 0; i < localStorage.length; i++) {
7766:                    const key = localStorage.key(i);
7767:                    if (!key) continue;
7768:                    allLocalData[key] = localStorage.getItem(key);
7769:                }
7770:                const backupTimestamp = new Date().toISOString();
7771:                localStorage.setItem('muller_last_backup_iso', backupTimestamp);
7772:                setLastBackupIso(backupTimestamp);
7773:                const dataToExport = {
7774:                    allLocalStorage: allLocalData,
7775:                    version: '4.0',
7776:                    exportDate: backupTimestamp
7777:                };
7778:                const blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify(dataToExport, null, 2)], {type: 'application/json'});
7779:                const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
7780:                const a = document.createElement('a');
7781:                a.href = url;
7782:                a.download = `muller_progreso_${new Date().toISOString().slice(0,19)}.json`;
7783:                a.click();
7784:                URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
7785:                window.__mullerToast && window.__mullerToast('Backup total exportado. Guárdalo para sincronizar.', 'success');
7786:            }, []);
7787:
7788:            React.useEffect(() => {
7789:                const onFull = () => exportData();
7790:                window.addEventListener('muller-export-full-backup', onFull);
7791:                return () => window.removeEventListener('muller-export-full-backup', onFull);
7792:            }, [exportData]);
7793:
7794:            const importData = (event) => {
7795:                const file = event.target.files[0];
7796:                if (!file) return;
7797:                const reader = new FileReader();
7798:                reader.onload = (e) => {
7799:                    try {
7800:                        const data = JSON.parse(e.target.result);
7801:                        if (data.type === 'muller_partial_v1' && data.part === 'srs') {
7802:                            localStorage.setItem('muller_vocab_srs_v1', JSON.stringify(data.muller_vocab_srs_v1 || {}));
7803:                            window.__mullerToast && window.__mullerToast('SRS importado. Recargando…', 'success');
7804:                            window.location.reload();
7805:                            return;
7806:                        }
7807:                        if (data.type === 'muller_partial_v1' && data.part === 'decks') {
7808:                            const cur = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('mullerStats') || '{}');
7809:                            const merged = { ...cur, difficultVocab: data.difficultVocab || cur.difficultVocab, normalVocab: data.normalVocab || cur.normalVocab, difficultGrammar: data.difficultGrammar || cur.difficultGrammar };
7810:                            localStorage.setItem('mullerStats', JSON.stringify(merged));
7811:                            window.__mullerToast && window.__mullerToast('Mazos importados. Recargando…', 'success');
7812:                            window.location.reload();
7813:                            return;
7814:                        }
7815:                        if (data.allLocalStorage && typeof data.allLocalStorage === 'object') {
7816:                            localStorage.clear();
7817:                            Object.entries(data.allLocalStorage).forEach(([key, value]) => {
7818:                                localStorage.setItem(key, value);
7819:                            });
7820:                            setLastBackupIso(localStorage.getItem('muller_last_backup_iso'));
7821:                        } else if (data.allMullerData && typeof data.allMullerData === 'object') {
7822:                            Object.entries(data.allMullerData).forEach(([key, value]) => {
7823:                                localStorage.setItem(key, value);
7824:                            });
7825:                            setLastBackupIso(localStorage.getItem('muller_last_backup_iso'));
7826:                        } else {
7827:                            if (data.userStats) localStorage.setItem('mullerStats', JSON.stringify(data.userStats));
7828:                            if (data.savedScripts) localStorage.setItem('mullerScripts', JSON.stringify(data.savedScripts));
7829:                            if (data.customVocabLessons) localStorage.setItem('mullerCustomVocab', JSON.stringify(data.customVocabLessons));
7830:                        }
7831:                        window.__mullerToast && window.__mullerToast('Datos importados correctamente. Recargando…', 'success');
7832:                        window.location.reload();
7833:                    } catch(err) { window.__mullerToast && window.__mullerToast('Archivo inválido.', 'error'); }
7834:                };
7835:                reader.readAsText(file);
7836:            };
7837:
7838:            const exportSrsOnly = () => {
7839:                try {
7840:                    const raw = localStorage.getItem('muller_vocab_srs_v1');
7841:                    const map = raw ? JSON.parse(raw) : {};
7842:                    const payload = { type: 'muller_partial_v1', part: 'srs', muller_vocab_srs_v1: map, exportDate: new Date().toISOString() };
7843:                    const blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify(payload, null, 2)], { type: 'application/json' });
7844:                    const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
7845:                    const a = document.createElement('a');
7846:                    a.href = url;
7847:                    a.download = `muller_srs_only_${new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 19)}.json`;
7848:                    a.click();
7849:                    URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
7850:                    window.__mullerToast && window.__mullerToast('Exportado solo SRS.', 'success');
7851:                } catch (err) { window.__mullerToast && window.__mullerToast('No se pudo exportar SRS.', 'error'); }
7852:            };
7853:
7854:            const exportDecksOnly = () => {
7855:                try {
7856:                    const stats = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('mullerStats') || '{}');
7857:                    const payload = {
7858:                        type: 'muller_partial_v1',
7859:                        part: 'decks',
7860:                        exportDate: new Date().toISOString(),
7861:                        difficultVocab: stats.difficultVocab || [],
7862:                        normalVocab: stats.normalVocab || [],
7863:                        difficultGrammar: stats.difficultGrammar || []
7864:                    };
7865:                    const blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify(payload, null, 2)], { type: 'application/json' });
7866:                    const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
7867:                    const a = document.createElement('a');
7868:                    a.href = url;
7869:                    a.download = `muller_mazos_${new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 19)}.json`;
7870:                    a.click();
7871:                    URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
7872:                    window.__mullerToast && window.__mullerToast('Exportados mazos (difícil/normal/gramática).', 'success');
7873:                } catch (err) { window.__mullerToast && window.__mullerToast('No se pudo exportar mazos.', 'error'); }
7874:            };
7875:
7876:            const showSyncHelp = () => {
7877:                alert(
7878:                    "🔄 Sincronización TOTAL gratis:\n\n" +
7879:                    "1) En tu dispositivo actual pulsa Exportar.\n" +
7880:                    "2) Sube el archivo .json a Google Drive.\n" +
7881:                    "3) En otro dispositivo descarga ese .json.\n" +
7882:                    "4) Pulsa Importar en la app.\n" +
7883:                    "5) Recarga la página.\n\n" +
7884:                    "Esto copia TODO el estado guardado de la aplicación."
7885:                );
7886:            };
7887:
7888:            React.useEffect(() => {
7889:                const onImport = () => {
7890:                    const el = document.getElementById('muller-backup-file-input');
7891:                    if (el) el.click();
7892:                };
7893:                const onSrs = () => exportSrsOnly();
7894:                const onDecks = () => exportDecksOnly();
7895:                const onHelp = () => showSyncHelp();
7896:                const onMic = () => requestMicPermission();
7897:                window.addEventListener('muller-open-backup-import', onImport);
7898:                window.addEventListener('muller-export-srs-only', onSrs);
7899:                window.addEventListener('muller-export-decks-only', onDecks);
7900:                window.addEventListener('muller-show-sync-help', onHelp);
7901:                window.addEventListener('muller-request-mic', onMic);
7902:                return () => {
7903:                    window.removeEventListener('muller-open-backup-import', onImport);
7904:                    window.removeEventListener('muller-export-srs-only', onSrs);
7905:                    window.removeEventListener('muller-export-decks-only', onDecks);
7906:                    window.removeEventListener('muller-show-sync-help', onHelp);
7907:                    window.removeEventListener('muller-request-mic', onMic);
7908:                };
7909:            }, [exportDecksOnly, exportSrsOnly]);
7910:
7911:            React.useEffect(() => {
7912:                let enable = false;
7913:                try { enable = localStorage.getItem(MULLER_MIC_PERMISSION_PREF_KEY) !== '0'; } catch (e) {}
7914:                if (!enable) return undefined;
7915:                const t = window.setTimeout(() => { requestMicPermission(); }, 600);
7916:                return () => window.clearTimeout(t);
7917:            }, []);
7918:
7919:            return (
7920:                <>
7921:                    <input id="muller-backup-file-input" type="file" accept=".json" onChange={importData} className="hidden" />
7922:                </>
7923:            );
7924:        }
7925:
7926:      const hidePreboot = () => {
7927:        const el = document.getElementById('muller-preboot');
7928:        if (!el) return;
7929:        el.classList.add('is-hidden');
7930:        window.setTimeout(() => {
7931:          try { if (el && el.parentNode) el.parentNode.removeChild(el); } catch (e) {}
7932:        }, 260);
7933:      };
7934:      const root = ReactDOM.createRoot(document.getElementById('root'));
7935:        root.render(
7936:            <MullerErrorBoundary>
7937:                <>

7941:                </>

7944:      window.requestAnimationFrame(() => window.requestAnimationFrame(hidePreboot));

7956:        if ('serviceWorker' in navigator) {
7957:            window.addEventListener('load', function () {
7958:                navigator.serviceWorker.getRegistrations()
7959:                    .then(function (regs) {
7960:                        return Promise.all(regs.map(function (reg) { return reg.unregister(); }));
7961:                    })
7962:                    .catch(function () {})
7963:                    .finally(function () {
7964:                        navigator.serviceWorker.register('./sw.js').catch(function () {});
7965:                    });
